#-------------------------------------------------------------------
# A2744 Spectroscopic Redshift Compilation.
# Benotto P. - Last compiled 2026-05-26
# Please always refer to the latest version of this catalogue: 
# https://pietrobenotto.github.io/research/A2744_redshift_compilation.txt
#
# This catalog compiles spectroscopic redshifts for the A2744 field.
# Redshifts within a 20' radius centered on the cluster are kept.
# The redshifts come from the following surveys:
#
#   - ASTRODEEP-JWST          (Merlin et al. 2024)
#   - UNCOVER                 (Prince et al. 2024)
#   - All the Little Things   (ALT, Naidu et al. 2024)
#   - NIRISS                  (Watson et al. 2025)
#   - DJA redshift compilation (Brammer & Valentino 2025,
#                               https://zenodo.org/records/15472354)
#                               v4.4, grade == 3 only
#   - MUSE surveys compilation:
#       Owers et al. 2011, Braglia et al. 2009, GLASS,
#       Richard et al. 2021, Bergamini et al. 2022,
#       Caminha MUSE DDT 2022, MUSE 2025 (PI: Matthee)
#-------------------------------------------------------------------
# ( 1)  RA           [Right Ascension J2000 (deg)]
#                       Right ascension from the same catalogue as the redshift.
# ( 2)  DEC          [Declination J2000 (deg)]
#                       Declination from the same catalogue as the redshift.
# ( 3)  ID           [Source identifier]
#                       Source identifier. A plain number is the ASTRODEEP ID of the
#                       nearest match within 1 arcsec. If no match exists, the original
#                       catalogue number is kept with a 3-letter prefix indicating its
#                       source. If multiple objects with different redshifts map to the
#                       same ID, a letter suffix is appended (_a, _b, ...).
# ( 4)  zspec        [Spectroscopic redshift]
#                       Spectroscopic redshift. If multiple sources lie within 1 arcsec
#                       and agree within 5% in redshift, only one entry is retained.
# ( 5)  source       [Origin of the redshift value]
# ( 6)  F090W_mag    [JWST/NIRCam F090W (AB magnitude)]
#                       ASTRODEEP KRON flux. -99 if no photometry available.
# ( 7)  F200W_mag    [JWST/NIRCam F200W (AB magnitude)]
#                       ASTRODEEP KRON flux. -99 if no photometry available.
# ( 8)  F444W_mag    [JWST/NIRCam F444W (AB magnitude)]
#                       ASTRODEEP KRON flux. -99 if no photometry available.
#-------------------------------------------------------------------
